---
title: Graphics
description: Animations in SplashKit can be used to move between cells in bitmaps and sprites. Each animation generates a number sequence that can then be used when drawing bitmaps.
---
:::tip[Graphics]
SplashKit Text allows for drawing text in a variety of ways to graphic windows.SplashKit Images allow drawing of bitmaps and sprites to graphic windows.
:::

import { Tabs, TabItem } from "@astrojs/starlight/components";

import { Code } from "astro/components";

## Functions
##
## Draw Circle [🧬](#group-draw-circle)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Draw Circle** (clr: color, c: circle )](/components/graphics/#draw-circle--1)
- [**Draw Circle** (clr: color, c: circle, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#draw-circle--2)
- [**Draw Circle** (clr: color, x: double, y: double, radius: double )](/components/graphics/#draw-circle--3)
- [**Draw Circle** (clr: color, x: double, y: double, radius: double, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#draw-circle--4)

:::

### Draw Circle [🤖](#draw-circle--1) 
Draw a circle on the current window. The circle is centred on its x, y
coordinates, and has the provided radius.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| clr | [`Color`](/components/types/#color) | The color of the circle |
| c | [`Circle`](/components/types/#circle) | The circle being drawn |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void draw_circle(color clr, const circle &c)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public void Circle.DrawCircle(Color clr);
public static void SplashKit.DrawCircle(Color clr, Circle c);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def draw_circle_record(clr, c):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure DrawCircle(clr: Color; const c: Circle)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
### Draw Circle [🤖](#draw-circle--2) 
Draw a circle with the provided drawing options, which may include options related to
the drawing destination.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| clr | [`Color`](/components/types/#color) | The color of the circle |
| c | [`Circle`](/components/types/#circle) | The circle being drawn |
| opts | [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) | Drawing options to configure the drawing operation |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void draw_circle(color clr, const circle &c, drawing_options opts)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public void Circle.DrawCircle(Color clr, DrawingOptions opts);
public static void SplashKit.DrawCircle(Color clr, Circle c, DrawingOptions opts);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def draw_circle_record_with_options(clr, c, opts):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure DrawCircle(clr: Color; const c: Circle; opts: DrawingOptions)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
### Draw Circle [🤖](#draw-circle--3) 
Draw a circle onto the current window. The circle is centred on its x, y
coordinates, and has the provided radius.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| clr | [`Color`](/components/types/#color) | The color of the circle |
| x | `Double` | The x location of the circle |
| y | `Double` | The y location of the circle |
| radius | `Double` | The radius of the circle |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void draw_circle(color clr, double x, double y, double radius)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static void SplashKit.DrawCircle(Color clr, double x, double y, double radius);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def draw_circle(clr, x, y, radius):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure DrawCircle(clr: Color; x: Double; y: Double; radius: Double)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
### Draw Circle [🤖](#draw-circle--4) 
Draw a circle using the supplied drawing options. The circle is centred on its x, y
coordinates, and has the provided radius. This will use [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) to determine
the destination.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| clr | [`Color`](/components/types/#color) | The color of the circle |
| x | `Double` | The x location of the circle |
| y | `Double` | The y location of the circle |
| radius | `Double` | The radius of the circle |
| opts | [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) | Drawing options to configure the drawing operation |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void draw_circle(color clr, double x, double y, double radius, drawing_options opts)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static void SplashKit.DrawCircle(Color clr, double x, double y, double radius, DrawingOptions opts);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def draw_circle_with_options(clr, x, y, radius, opts):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure DrawCircle(clr: Color; x: Double; y: Double; radius: Double; opts: DrawingOptions)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
## Draw Circle On Bitmap [🧬](#group-draw-circle-on-bitmap)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Draw Circle On Bitmap** (destination: bitmap, clr: color, x: double, y: double, radius: double )](/components/graphics/#draw-circle-on-bitmap--1)
- [**Draw Circle On Bitmap** (destination: bitmap, clr: color, x: double, y: double, radius: double, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#draw-circle-on-bitmap--2)

:::

### Draw Circle On Bitmap [🤖](#draw-circle-on-bitmap--1) 
Draw a circle onto the destination bitmap. The circle is centred on its x, y
coordinates, and has the provided radius.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| destination | [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) | The destination bitmap |
| clr | [`Color`](/components/types/#color) | The color of the circle |
| x | `Double` | The x location of the circle |
| y | `Double` | The y location of the circle |
| radius | `Double` | The radius of the circle |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void draw_circle_on_bitmap(bitmap destination, color clr, double x, double y, double radius)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public void Bitmap.DrawCircleOnBitmap(Color clr, double x, double y, double radius);
public static void SplashKit.DrawCircleOnBitmap(Bitmap destination, Color clr, double x, double y, double radius);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def draw_circle_on_bitmap(destination, clr, x, y, radius):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure DrawCircleOnBitmap(destination: Bitmap; clr: Color; x: Double; y: Double; radius: Double)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
### Draw Circle On Bitmap [🤖](#draw-circle-on-bitmap--2) 
Draw a circle to the bitmap using the supplied drawing options. The circle is centred on its x, y
coordinates, and has the provided radius.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| destination | [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) | The destination bitmap |
| clr | [`Color`](/components/types/#color) | The color of the circle |
| x | `Double` | The x location of the circle |
| y | `Double` | The y location of the circle |
| radius | `Double` | The radius of the circle |
| opts | [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) | Drawing options to configure the drawing operation |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void draw_circle_on_bitmap(bitmap destination, color clr, double x, double y, double radius, drawing_options opts)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public void Bitmap.DrawCircleOnBitmap(Color clr, double x, double y, double radius, DrawingOptions opts);
public static void SplashKit.DrawCircleOnBitmap(Bitmap destination, Color clr, double x, double y, double radius, DrawingOptions opts);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def draw_circle_on_bitmap_with_options(destination, clr, x, y, radius, opts):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure DrawCircleOnBitmap(destination: Bitmap; clr: Color; x: Double; y: Double; radius: Double; opts: DrawingOptions)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

## Draw Text [🧬](#group-draw-text)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Draw Text** (text: string, clr: color, fnt: string, font_size: int, x: double, y: double )](/components/graphics/#draw-text--1)
- [**Draw Text** (text: string, clr: color, fnt: string, font_size: int, x: double, y: double, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#draw-text--2)

- [**Draw Text** (text: string, clr: color, x: double, y: double, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#draw-text--4)
- [**Draw Text** (text: string, clr: color, fnt: font, font_size: int, x: double, y: double )](/components/graphics/#draw-text--5)
- [**Draw Text** (text: string, clr: color, fnt: font, font_size: int, x: double, y: double, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#draw-text--6)

:::

| fnt | `String` | The name of the [`Font`](/components/types/#font) which will be used to draw the text |
| font_size | `Integer` | The size of the font which will be drawn. |
| x | `Double` | The x location to draw the text. |
| y | `Double` | The y location to draw the text. |

## Draw Text On Window [🧬](#group-draw-text-on-window)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Draw Text On Window** (wnd: window, text: string, clr: color, fnt: string, font_size: int, x: double, y: double )](/components/graphics/#draw-text-on-window--1)
- [**Draw Text On Window** (wnd: window, text: string, clr: color, fnt: string, font_size: int, x: double, y: double, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#draw-text-on-window--2)
- [**Draw Text On Window** (wnd: window, text: string, clr: color, x: double, y: double )](/components/graphics/#draw-text-on-window--3)
- [**Draw Text On Window** (wnd: window, text: string, clr: color, x: double, y: double, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#draw-text-on-window--4)
- [**Draw Text On Window** (wnd: window, text: string, clr: color, fnt: font, font_size: int, x: double, y: double )](/components/graphics/#draw-text-on-window--5)
- [**Draw Text On Window** (wnd: window, text: string, clr: color, fnt: font, font_size: int, x: double, y: double, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#draw-text-on-window--6)

:::

### Draw Text On Window [🤖](#draw-text-on-window--1) 
**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| wnd | window | The window to draw to |
| text | `String` | The text string to be written to the window. |
| clr | [`Color`](/components/types/#color) | The desired [`Color`](/components/types/#color) of the text to be written. |
| fnt | `String` | The name of the [`Font`](/components/types/#font) which will be used to draw the text |
| font_size | `Integer` | The size of the font which will be drawn. |
| x | `Double` | The x location to draw the text. |
| y | `Double` | The y location to draw the text. |

**Signatures**

Draw a rectangle to the bitmap using the supplied rect. The rectangle is centred on its x, y

### Draw Rectangle On Bitmap [🤖](#draw-rectangle-on-bitmap--4) 
Draw a rectangle to the bitmap using the supplied drawing options. The rectangle is centred on its x, y
coordinates, and has the provided width and height.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| destination | [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) | The destination bitmap |
| clr | [`Color`](/components/types/#color) | The color of the rectangle |
| x | `Double` | The x location of the rectangle |
| y | `Double` | The y location of the rectangle |
| width | `Double` | The width of the rectangle |
| height | `Double` | The height of the rectangle |
| opts | [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) | Drawing options to configure the drawing operation |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">

## Push Clip [🧬](#group-push-clip)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Push Clip** (wnd: window, r: rectangle )](/components/graphics/#push-clip--1)
- [**Push Clip** (bmp: bitmap, r: rectangle )](/components/graphics/#push-clip--2)
- [**Push Clip** (r: rectangle )](/components/graphics/#push-clip--3)

:::

### Push Clip [🤖](#push-clip--1) 
Add the clipping rectangle of a window and uses the intersect between
the new rectangle and previous clip.

When a clipping rectangle is provided, drawing operations will only
affect the area specified in the current clipping rectangle.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| wnd | window | The window to add clipping to |
| r | [`Rectangle`](/components/types/#rectangle) | The new clipping rectangle |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void push_clip(window wnd, const rectangle &r)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static void SplashKit.PushClip(Window wnd, Rectangle r);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def push_clip_for_window(wnd, r):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure PushClip(wnd: Window; const r: Rectangle)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
### Push Clip [🤖](#push-clip--2) 
Add the clipping rectangle of a bitmap and uses the intersect between
the new rectangle and previous clip.

When a clipping rectangle is provided, drawing operations will only
affect the area specified in the current clipping rectangle.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| bmp | [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) | The bitmap to add clipping to |
| r | [`Rectangle`](/components/types/#rectangle) | The new clipping rectangle |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void push_clip(bitmap bmp, const rectangle &r)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static void SplashKit.PushClip(Bitmap bmp, Rectangle r);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def push_clip_for_bitmap(bmp, r):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure PushClip(bmp: Bitmap; const r: Rectangle)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
### Push Clip [🤖](#push-clip--3) 
Push a clip rectangle to the current window. The resulting clipping
rectangle will be the intersection of the existing clipping rectangle
with the new rectangle provided in this call. This can be undone using
`pop_clip`.

When a clipping rectangle is provided, drawing operations will only
affect the area specified in the current clipping rectangle.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| r | [`Rectangle`](/components/types/#rectangle) | The new clipping rectangle |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void push_clip(const rectangle &r)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static void SplashKit.PushClip(Rectangle r);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def push_clip(r):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure PushClip(const r: Rectangle)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

## Set Clip [🧬](#group-set-clip)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Set Clip** (r: rectangle )](/components/graphics/#set_clip--1)
- [**Set Clip** (bmp: bitmap, r: rectangle )](/components/graphics/#set-clip--2)
- [**Set Clip** (wnd: window, r: rectangle )](/components/graphics/#set-clip--3)

:::

### Set Clip [🤖](#set-clip--1) 
Set the clip rectangle of the current window. This will clear any
existing clipping rectangles pushed to the current window, and use the
supplied rectangle for clipping.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| r | [`Rectangle`](/components/types/#rectangle) | The new clipping rectangle |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void set_clip(const rectangle &r)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">

### Set Clip [🤖](#set-clip--2) 
Set the clip rectangle of the bitmap. This will clear any existing
clipping rectangles pushed to the bitmap, and use the supplied rectangle
for clipping.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| bmp | [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) | The bitmap to change |
| r | [`Rectangle`](/components/types/#rectangle) | The new clipping rectangle |

## Fill Triangle [🧬](#group-fill-triangle)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Fill Triangle** (clr: color, tri: triangle )](/components/graphics/#fill_triangle--1)
- [**Fill Triangle** (clr: color, tri: triangle, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#fill-triangle--2)
- [**Fill Triangle** (clr: color, x1: double, y1: double, x2: double, y2: double, x3: double, y3: double )](/components/graphics/#fill-triangle--3)
- [**Fill Triangle** (clr: color, x1: double, y1: double, x2: double, y2: double, x3: double, y3: double, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#fill-triangle--4)

:::

### Fill Triangle [🤖](#fill-triangle--1)

- `Void`

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| clr | [`Color`](/components/types/#color) | The color for the triangle |
| tri | [`Triangle`](/components/types/#triangle) | The triangles details |

second point of the triangle |
| y2 | `Double` | The distance from the top of the window to the
second point of the triangle |

  </TabItem>

### Draw Ellipse [🤖](#draw-ellipse--2) 
Draws an ellipse using the provided location, size, and drawing options.

At this stage ellipse drawing is not affected by line width from the
drawing options.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| clr | [`Color`](/components/types/#color) | The color of the ellipse |
| rect | [`Rectangle`](/components/types/#rectangle) | Indicates the location and size of the ellipse |
| opts | [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) | The drawing options |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void draw_ellipse(color clr, const rectangle rect, drawing_options opts)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static void SplashKit.DrawEllipse(Color clr, Rectangle rect, DrawingOptions opts);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def draw_ellipse_within_rectangle_with_options(clr, rect, opts):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure DrawEllipse(clr: Color; rect: Rectangle; opts: DrawingOptions)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

### Draw Ellipse [🤖](#draw-ellipse--3)

### Fill Ellipse On Bitmap [🤖](#fill-ellipse-on-bitmap--2) 
Fills an ellipse on the given bitmap, using the provided location, size, and drawing options.

At this stage ellipse drawing is not affected by line width from the
drawing options.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| destination | [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) | the bitmap to draw the ellipse on |
| clr | [`Color`](/components/types/#color) | The color of the ellipse |
| rect | [`Rectangle`](/components/types/#rectangle) | Indicates the location and size of the ellipse |
| opts | [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) | The drawing options |

| y | `Double` | The distance from the top of the bitmap or bitmap to the

| height | `Double` | The height of the ellipse |

## Bitmap Set Cell Details [🔗](#bitmap-set-cell-details)

 
Initialise the bitmap cell details. This allows parts of the bitmap to be
drawn as individual cells.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| bmp | [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) | The bitmap |
| width | `Integer` | The width of each cell |
| height | `Integer` | The height of each cell |
| columns | `Integer` | The number of cell columns within the bitmap |
| rows | `Integer` | The number of cell rows within the bitmap |
| count | `Integer` | The total number of cells, may be fewer than columns *
rows |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void bitmap_set_cell_details(bitmap bmp, int width, int height, int columns, int rows, int count)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public void Bitmap.BitmapSetCellDetails(int width, int height, int columns, int rows, int count);
public static void SplashKit.BitmapSetCellDetails(Bitmap bmp, int width, int height, int columns, int rows, int count);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def bitmap_set_cell_details(bmp, width, height, columns, rows, count):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure BitmapSetCellDetails(bmp: Bitmap; width: Integer; height: Integer; columns: Integer; rows: Integer; count: Integer)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

## Create Bitmap [🔗](#create-bitmap)

 
Creates a new bitmap that you can draw to. Initially the bitmap will
be transparent.

**Return Type**

- [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| name | `String` | The name of the bitmap resource to be created. If this
already exists SplashKit will alter the name to make it
unique. |
| width | `Integer` | The width of the created bitmap |
| height | `Integer` | The height of the created bitmap |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`bitmap create_bitmap(string name, int width, int height)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static Bitmap SplashKit.CreateBitmap(string name, int width, int height);

  </TabItem>

## Draw Bitmap [🧬](#group-draw-bitmap)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Draw Bitmap** (bmp: bitmap, x: double, y: double )](/components/graphics/#draw-bitmap--1)
- [**Draw Bitmap** (bmp: bitmap, x: double, y: double, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#draw-bitmap--2)
- [**Draw Bitmap** (name: string, x: double, y: double )](/components/graphics/#draw-bitmap--3)
- [**Draw Bitmap** (name: string, x: double, y: double, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#draw-bitmap--4)

:::

### Draw Bitmap [🤖](#draw-bitmap--1) 
Draws the bitmap supplied into `bmp` to the current window.
at `x` and `y`.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| bmp | [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) | the bitmap which will be drawn to the screen |
| x | `Double` | the x location which represents where the bitmap
will be drawn |
| y | `Double` | the y location which represents where the bitmap
will be drawn |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void draw_bitmap(bitmap bmp, double x, double y)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public void Bitmap.DrawBitmap(double x, double y);
public static void SplashKit.DrawBitmap(Bitmap bmp, double x, double y);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def draw_bitmap(bmp, x, y):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure DrawBitmap(bmp: Bitmap; x: Double; y: Double)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
### Draw Bitmap [🤖](#draw-bitmap--2) 
Draws the bitmap supplied into `bmp` to the current window.
with extra drawing options supplied in `opts` at `x` and `y`.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| bmp | [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) | the bitmap which will be drawn to the screen |
| x | `Double` | the x location which represents where the bitmap
will be drawn |
| y | `Double` | the y location which represents where the bitmap
will be drawn |
| opts | [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) | the [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) which provide extra information
for how to draw the [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void draw_bitmap(bitmap bmp, double x, double y, drawing_options opts)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public void Bitmap.DrawBitmap(double x, double y, DrawingOptions opts);
public static void SplashKit.DrawBitmap(Bitmap bmp, double x, double y, DrawingOptions opts);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def draw_bitmap_with_options(bmp, x, y, opts):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure DrawBitmap(bmp: Bitmap; x: Double; y: Double; opts: DrawingOptions)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---

  </TabItem>

### Draw Bitmap [🤖](#draw-bitmap--4)

with extra drawing options supplied in `opts` at `x` and `y`.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| name | `String` | the name of the bitmap which will be drawn to the screen |
| x | `Double` | the x location which represents where the bitmap
will be drawn |
| y | `Double` | the y location which represents where the bitmap
will be drawn |
| opts | [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) | the [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) which provide extra information
for how to draw the [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void draw_bitmap(string name, double x, double y, drawing_options opts)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static void Images.DrawBitmap(string name, double x, double y, DrawingOptions opts);
public static void SplashKit.DrawBitmap(string name, double x, double y, DrawingOptions opts);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def draw_bitmap_named_with_options(name, x, y, opts):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure DrawBitmap(name: String; x: Double; y: Double; opts: DrawingOptions)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
## Load Bitmap [🔗](#load-bitmap)

 
Loads and returns a bitmap. The supplied `filename` is used to
locate the Bitmap to load. The supplied `name` indicates the
name to use to refer to this Bitmap in SplashKit. The [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) can then
be retrieved by passing this `name` to the `bitmap_named` function.

**Return Type**

- [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| name | `String` | The name of the bitmap resource in SplashKit |
| filename | `String` | The filename to load |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`bitmap load_bitmap(string name, string filename)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static Bitmap SplashKit.LoadBitmap(string name, string filename);
public Bitmap(string name, string filename);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def load_bitmap(name, filename):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`function LoadBitmap(name: String; filename: String): Bitmap`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

## Setup Collision Mask [🔗](#setup-collision-mask)

 
Sets up the collision mask for a bitmap. This enables collision detection between
this bitmap and other bitmaps or shapes.

This is automatically called when a bitmap is loaded, and only needs to be 
called on bitmaps created using `create_bitmap`, and when a bitmap is
changed by drawing onto the bitmap.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| bmp | [`Bitmap`](/components/types/#bitmap) | the bitmap to setup |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void setup_collision_mask(bitmap bmp)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public void Bitmap.SetupCollisionMask();
public static void SplashKit.SetupCollisionMask(Bitmap bmp);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def setup_collision_mask(bmp):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure SetupCollisionMask(bmp: Bitmap)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

| x1 | `Double` | The distance from the left of the window/bitmap to the first
point |
| y1 | `Double` | The distance from the top of the window/bitmap to the first
point |
| x2 | `Double` | The distance from the left of the window/bitmap to the second
point |
| y2 | `Double` | The distance from the top of the window/bitmap to the second
point |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">

  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">

- [**Draw Line On Bitmap** (destination: bitmap, clr: color, from_pt: point_2d, to_pt: point_2d )](/components/graphics/#draw-line-on-bitmap--3)

## Option Defaults [🔗](#option-defaults)

 
Returns a [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) with default values.
This will draw to the current window, with default scale of 1, no
rotation or offset, not flipped, drawing whole images, with default
camera mechanisms and line width.

**Return Type**

- [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) 

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`drawing_options option_defaults()`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static DrawingOptions SplashKit.OptionDefaults();`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def option_defaults():`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`function OptionDefaults(): DrawingOptions`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
## Option Draw To [🧬](#group-option-draw-to)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Option Draw To** (dest: bitmap )](/components/graphics/#option-draw-to--1)
- [**Option Draw To** (dest: bitmap, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#option-draw-to--2)
- [**Option Draw To** (dest: window )](/components/graphics/#option-draw-to--3)
- [**Option Draw To** (dest: window, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#optio-draw-to--4)

:::

### Option Draw To [🤖](#option-draw-to--1)

### Option Scale Bmp [🤖](#option-scale-bmp--2) 
Use this option to scale the drawing of bitmaps. You can scale x and y separately.
Pass opts the other options you want use.

**Return Type**

- [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| scale_x | `Double` | The amount to scale bitmaps aalong the x axis |
| scale_y | `Double` | The amount to scale bitmaps aalong the y axis |
| opts | [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) | Values for the other options. |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`drawing_options option_scale_bmp(double scale_x, double scale_y, drawing_options opts)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static DrawingOptions SplashKit.OptionScaleBmp(double scaleX, double scaleY, DrawingOptions opts);`} lang="csharp" />

## Option With Bitmap Cell [🧬](#group-option-with-bitmap-cell)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Option With Bitmap Cell** (cell: int )](/components/graphics/#option-with-bitmap_cell--1)
- [**Option With Bitmap Cell** (cell: int, opts: drawing_options )](/components/graphics/#option-with-bitmap-cell--2)

:::

### Option With Bitmap Cell [🤖](#option-with-bitmap-cell--1) 
When drawing the bitmap this will only draw the cell. To use this the bitmap
needs to have been provided with its cell details (see `bitmap_set_cell_details`).
This option overrides the animation or part drawing options.

**Return Type**

- [`Drawing Options`](/components/types/#drawing-options) 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| cell | `Integer` | The cell to draw from the bitmap (-1 for entire bitmap) |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`drawing_options option_with_bitmap_cell(int cell)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static DrawingOptions SplashKit.OptionWithBitmapCell(int cell);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def option_with_bitmap_cell(cell):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`function OptionWithBitmapCell(cell: Integer): DrawingOptions`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
### Option With Bitmap Cell [🤖](#option-with-bitmap-cell--2) 
When drawing the bitmap this will only draw the cell. To use this the bitmap
needs to have been provided with its cell details (see `bitmap_set_cell_details`).
This option overrides the animation or part drawing options. This extends
the passed in drawing options with the cell details.

**Return Type**

### Refresh Screen [🤖](#refresh-screen--2) 
Refreshes all open windows with a target FPS (frames per second). This will
delay a period of time that will approximately meet the targeted frames per
second.

**Return Type**

- `Void`

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| target_fps | unsigned int | The targeted frames per second to refresh the screen at. |

  </TabItem>

  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">

  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure RefreshScreen(targetFps: Cardinal)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>

## Take Screenshot [🧬](#group-take-screenshot)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Take Screenshot** (basename: string )](/components/graphics/#take-screenshot--1)
- [**Take Screenshot** (wind: window, basename: string )](/components/graphics/#take-screenshot--2)

### Take Screenshot [🤖](#take-screenshot--1) 
Saves a screenshot of the current window to a bitmap file. The file will
be saved onto the user's desktop.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| basename | `String` | The base of the filename. If there is a file of this name
already, then the name will be changed to generate a
unique filename. |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void take_screenshot(const string &basename)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static void SplashKit.TakeScreenshot(string basename);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def take_screenshot(basename):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure TakeScreenshot(const basename: String)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
### Take Screenshot [🤖](#take-screenshot--2) 
Saves a screenshot of the current window to a bitmap file. The file will
be saved onto the user's desktop.

**Return Type**

- `Void` 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| wind | window | The window to capture in the screenshot |
| basename | `String` | The base of the filename. If there is a file of this name
already, then the name will be changed to generate a
unique filename. |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`void take_screenshot(window wind, const string &basename)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static void SplashKit.TakeScreenshot(Window wind, string basename);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def take_screenshot_of_window(wind, basename):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`procedure TakeScreenshot(wind: Window; const basename: String)`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

  </TabItem>

    <Code code={`function GetPixel(wnd: Window; const pt: Point2D): Color`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
### Get Pixel [🤖](#get-pixel--6) 
Returns the color of the pixel at the x,y location on the supplied
window.

**Return Type**

- [`Color`](/components/types/#color) 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| wnd | window | The window to get the color from |
| x | `Double` | The distance from the left edge of the window to the pixel
to read |
| y | `Double` | The distance from the top of the window to the pixel to read |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`color get_pixel(window wnd, double x, double y)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static Color SplashKit.GetPixel(Window wnd, double x, double y);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def get_pixel_from_window(wnd, x, y):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`function GetPixel(wnd: Window; x: Double; y: Double): Color`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

---
## Get Pixel From Window [🧬](#group-get-pixel-from-window)

:::note

This function is overloaded. The following versions exist:

- [**Get Pixel From Window** (destination: window, pt: point_2d )](/components/graphics/#get-pixel-from-window--1)
- [**Get Pixel From Window** (destination: window, x: double, y: double )](/components/graphics/#get-pixel-from-window--2)

:::

### Get Pixel From Window [🤖](#get-pixel-from-window--1) 
Returns the color of the pixel at the x,y location on the given
window.

**Return Type**

- [`Color`](/components/types/#color) 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| destination | window | The window to draw the pixel on |
| pt | [`Point 2D`](/components/types/#point-2d) | The position of the pixel |

**Signatures**

<Tabs>
  <TabItem label="C++">
    <Code code={`color get_pixel_from_window(window destination, const point_2d &pt)`} lang="cpp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="C#">
    <Code code={`public static Color SplashKit.GetPixelFromWindow(Window destination, Point2D pt);`} lang="csharp" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Python">
    <Code code={`def get_pixel_from_window_at_point_from_window(destination, pt):`} lang="python" />
  </TabItem>
  <TabItem label="Pascal">
    <Code code={`function GetPixelFromWindow(destination: Window; const pt: Point2D): Color`} lang="pascal" />
  </TabItem>
</Tabs>

### Get Pixel From Window [🤖](#get-pixel-from-window--2)

window.

**Return Type**

- [`Color`](/components/types/#color) 

**Parameters**

| Name   | Type                                               | Description                                                                        |
| ------ | -------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| destination | window | The window to draw the pixel on |
| x | `Double` | The distance from the left edge of the window to the pixel
to read |
| y | `Double` | The distance from the top of the window to the pixel to read |
